However, this regular expression does not specifically match strings that end with `@mysite.com`. It matches any string that contains an email address with a valid domain extension.  ## Analysis of Response B  Response B is: `^(.+@mysite.com)$`  Analysis: This regular expression is designed to match any string that ends with `@mysite.com`.
